Confidence Engine Integration\n\n**Unified Confidence Calculation:**\n\n```python\n# src/confidence_engine/murphy_validator.py (NEW)\nclass UnifiedConfidenceEngine:\n    """\n    Combines original G/D/H with new UD/UA/UI/UR/UG\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        # Original system\n        self.confidence_calculator = ConfidenceCalculator()  # G/D/H\n        self.phase_controller = PhaseController()\n        \n        # New system\n        self.uncertainty_calculator = UncertaintyCalculator()  # UD/UA/UI/UR/UG\n        self.murphy_gate = MurphyGate()\n    \n    def calculate_confidence(self, task):\n        # Get original confidence (G/D/H)\n        gdh_confidence = self.confidence_calculator.calculate(task)\n        \n        # Get new uncertainty scores\n        uncertainty = self.uncertainty_calculator.calculate(task)\n        \n        # Combine both approaches\n        final_confidence = self._merge_scores(gdh_confidence, uncertainty)\n        \n        # Apply Murphy Gate\n        gate_result = self.murphy_gate.evaluate(final_confidence, uncertainty)\n        \n        return gate_result\n```\n\n### 4. Execution Engine Integration\n\n**Form-Driven Execution with Existing Engine:**\n\n```python\n# src/execution_engine/form_executor.py (NEW)\nclass FormDrivenExecutor:\n    """\n    Executes form-submitted tasks using existing execution engine\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        # Use existing execution engine\n        from .execution_orchestrator import ExecutionOrchestrator\n        self.orchestrator = ExecutionOrchestrator()\n        \n        # Use existing phase controller\n        from ..confidence_engine.phase_controller import PhaseController\n        self.phase_controller = PhaseController()\n        \n        # Add new Murphy validation\n        from ..confidence_engine.murphy_validator import UnifiedConfidenceEngine\n        self.confidence_engine = UnifiedConfidenceEngine()\n    \n    async def execute_form_task(self, form_data):\n        # Convert form to task\n        task = self._form_to_task(form_data)\n        \n        # Validate with Murphy Gate\n        validation = self.confidence_engine.calculate_confidence(task)\n        \n        if not validation.approved:\n            return {"status": "rejected", "reason": validation.reason}\n        \n        # Execute using existing orchestrator\n        result = await self.orchestrator.execute(task)\n        \n        return result\n```\n\n### 5. Learning Engine Integration\n\n**Correction Capture with Existing Learning:**\n\n```python\n# src/learning_engine/correction_capture.py (NEW)\nclass IntegratedCorrectionSystem:\n    """\n    Captures corrections and feeds to existing learning engine\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        # Use existing learning engine\n        from .learning_system import LearningSystem\n        self.learning_system = LearningSystem()\n        \n        # Add new correction capture\n        self.correction_recorder = CorrectionRecorder()\n        self.feedback_system = FeedbackSystem()\n    \n    def capture_correction(self, task_id, correction_data):\n        # Record correction\n        correction = self.correction_recorder.record(task_id, correction_data)\n        \n        # Extract patterns\n        patterns = self._extract_patterns(correction)\n        \n        # Feed to existing learning engine\n        self.learning_system.learn_from_correction(patterns)\n        \n        # Train shadow agent\n        self._update_shadow_agent(correction)\n```\n\n### 6. Confidence Engine Integration\n**File:** `src/confidence_engine/murphy_validator.py`\n\n**Integrates:**\n- Existing: `confidence_calculator.py` (G/D/H formula)\n- New: `uncertainty_calculator.py` (UD/UA/UI/UR/UG)\n- New: `murphy_gate.py` (threshold decisions)\n\n**Strategy:**\n```python\nclass UnifiedConfidenceEngine:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Existing\n        self.confidence_calculator = ConfidenceCalculator()  # G/D/H\n        \n        # New\n        self.uncertainty_calculator = UncertaintyCalculator()  # UD/UA/UI/UR/UG\n        self.murphy_gate = MurphyGate()\n    \n    def calculate_confidence(self, task):\n        # Get both scores\n        gdh_score = self.confidence_calculator.calculate(task)\n        uncertainty_scores = self.uncertainty_calculator.calculate(task)\n        \n        # Merge and decide\n        final_score = self._merge_scores(gdh_score, uncertainty_scores)\n        gate_result = self.murphy_gate.evaluate(final_score, uncertainty_scores)\n        \n        return gate_result\n```\n\n### 2. Execution Engine Integration\n**File:** `src/execution_engine/form_executor.py`\n\n**Integrates:**\n- Existing: `execution_orchestrator.py`\n- Existing: `phase_controller.py` (from confidence_engine)\n- New: Form-driven execution\n\n**Strategy:**\n```python\nclass FormDrivenExecutor:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Use existing orchestrator\n        from .execution_orchestrator import ExecutionOrchestrator\n        self.orchestrator = ExecutionOrchestrator()\n        \n        # Use existing phase controller\n        from ..confidence_engine.phase_controller import PhaseController\n        self.phase_controller = PhaseController()\n        \n        # Add Murphy validation\n        from ..confidence_engine.murphy_validator import UnifiedConfidenceEngine\n        self.confidence_engine = UnifiedConfidenceEngine()\n    \n    async def execute_form_task(self, form_data):\n        # Convert form to task\n        task = self._form_to_task(form_data)\n        \n        # Validate with Murphy\n        validation = self.confidence_engine.calculate_confidence(task)\n        \n        if not validation.approved:\n            return {"status": "rejected"}\n        \n        # Execute with existing orchestrator\n        result = await self.orchestrator.execute(task)\n        \n        return result\n```\n\n### 3. Learning Engine Integration\n**File:** `src/learning_engine/correction_capture.py`\n\n**Integrates:**\n- Existing: `learning_system.py`\n- New: Correction capture and pattern extraction\n\n**Strategy:**\n```python\nclass IntegratedCorrectionSystem:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Use existing learning system\n        from .learning_system import LearningSystem\n        self.learning_system = LearningSystem()\n        \n        # Add new correction capture\n        self.correction_recorder = CorrectionRecorder()\n        self.pattern_extractor = PatternExtractor()\n    \n    def capture_correction(self, task_id, correction_data):\n        # Record correction\n        correction = self.correction_recorder.record(task_id, correction_data)\n        \n        # Extract patterns\n        patterns = self.pattern_extractor.extract(correction)\n        \n        # Feed to existing learning engine\n        self.learning_system.learn_from_correction(patterns)\n        \n        return correction\n```\n\n### 4. Supervisor Integration\n**File:** `src/supervisor_system/hitl_monitor.py`\n\n**Integrates:**\n- Existing: `supervisor_system/` modules\n- New: HITL checkpoints and interventions\n\n**Strategy:**\n```python\nclass IntegratedHITLMonitor:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Use existing supervisor\n        from .supervisor import Supervisor\n        self.supervisor = Supervisor()\n        \n        # Add HITL monitoring\n        self.hitl_monitor = HumanInTheLoopMonitor()\n    \n    def check_intervention_needed(self, task, phase):\n        # Check with existing supervisor\n        supervisor_decision = self.supervisor.should_intervene(task)\n        \n        # Check with HITL monitor\n        hitl_decision = self.hitl_monitor.check_checkpoint(task, phase)\n        \n        # Combine decisions\n        return supervisor_decision or hitl_decision\n```\n\n## File Count Summary\n\n### murphy_implementation (Source)\n- Total files: 54 Python files\n- Forms: 4 files\n- Plan: 3 files\n- Validation: 8 files\n- Risk: 6 files\n- Performance: 1 file\n- Execution: 4 files\n- HITL: 3 files\n- Correction: 7 files\n- Training: 3 files\n- Deployment: 15 files (not integrating - separate concern)\n\n### murphy_integrated (Target)\n- Existing: 272 Python files\n- Adding: ~39 Python files (excluding deployment)\n- Total after integration: ~311 Python files\n\n## Next Steps\n\n1. ✅ Create murphy_integrated/ workspace\n2. ✅ Copy murphy_backup_extracted to murphy_integrated\n3. Murphy Gate threshold-based validation\n    \n    This provides a comprehensive confidence assessment that uses both\n    the original proven approach and the new enhanced uncertainty analysis.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        """Initialize unified confidence engine"""\n        \n        # Original system components\n        if HAS_ORIGINAL_CALCULATOR:\n            self.confidence_calculator = ConfidenceCalculator()\n            logger.info("Loaded original ConfidenceCalculator (G/D/H)")\n        else:\n            self.confidence_calculator = None\n            logger.warning("Original ConfidenceCalculator not available")\n        \n        if HAS_PHASE_CONTROLLER:\n            self.phase_controller = PhaseController()\n            logger.info("Loaded original PhaseController")\n        else:\n            self.phase_controller = None\n            logger.warning("Original PhaseController not available")\n        \n        # New Murphy validation components\n        self.uncertainty_calculator = UncertaintyCalculator()\n        self.murphy_gate = MurphyGate()\n        \n        # Configuration\n        self.weights = {\n            \'gdh\': 0.5,  # Weight for original G/D/H score\n            \'uncertainty\': 0.5  # Weight for new uncertainty score\n        }\n        \n        logger.info("UnifiedConfidenceEngine initialized")\n    \n    def calculate_confidence(\n        self,\n        task: Dict[str, Any],\n        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> ConfidenceReport:\n        """\n        Calculate unified confidence score\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task to evaluate\n            context: Additional context (optional)\n        \n        Returns:\n            ConfidenceReport with combined scores and gate decision\n        """\n        \n        # Calculate original G/D/H confidence if available\n        gdh_confidence = None\n        if self.confidence_calculator:\n            try:\n                gdh_confidence = self.confidence_calculator.calculate(task)\n                logger.debug(f"G/D/H confidence: {gdh_confidence}")\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f"Error calculating G/D/H confidence: {e}")\n        \n        # Calculate new uncertainty scores\n        uncertainty_scores = self.uncertainty_calculator.calculate(task, context)\n        logger.debug(f"Uncertainty scores: {uncertainty_scores}")\n        \n        # Combine scores\n        if gdh_confidence is not None:\n            # Use weighted average of both approaches\n            combined_confidence = (\n                self.weights[\'gdh\'] * gdh_confidence +\n                self.weights[\'uncertainty\'] * (1.0 - uncertainty_scores.total)\n            )\n        else:\n            # Use only uncertainty-based confidence\n            combined_confidence = 1.0 - uncertainty_scores.total\n        \n        # Apply Murphy Gate\n        gate_result = self.murphy_gate.evaluate(\n            confidence=combined_confidence,\n            uncertainty_scores=uncertainty_scores,\n            task=task\n        )\n        \n        # Create comprehensive report\n        report = ConfidenceReport(\n            timestamp=datetime.now(),\n            task_id=task.get(\'id\', \'unknown\'),\n            gdh_confidence=gdh_confidence,\n            uncertainty_scores=uncertainty_scores,\n            combined_confidence=combined_confidence,\n            gate_result=gate_result,\n            metadata={\n                \'has_original_calculator\': HAS_ORIGINAL_CALCULATOR,\n                \'has_phase_controller\': HAS_PHASE_CONTROLLER,\n                \'weights\': self.weights\n            }\n        )\n        \n        logger.info(\n            f"Unified confidence for task {task.get(\'id\')}: "\n            f"{combined_confidence:.3f} (approved: {gate_result.approved})"\n        )\n        \n        return report\n    \n    def should_proceed(\n        self,\n        task: Dict[str, Any],\n        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> bool:\n        """\n        Determine if task should proceed based on confidence\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task to evaluate\n            context: Additional context\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if task should proceed, False otherwise\n        """\n        report = self.calculate_confidence(task, context)\n        return report.gate_result.approved\n    \n    def get_phase_recommendation(\n        self,\n        task: Dict[str, Any],\n        current_phase: str\n    ) -> str:\n        """\n        Get phase recommendation using original phase controller if available\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task being executed\n            current_phase: Current execution phase\n        \n        Returns:\n            Recommended next phase\n        """\n        if self.phase_controller:\n            try:\n                return self.phase_controller.get_next_phase(task, current_phase)\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f"Error getting phase recommendation: {e}")\n        \n        # Fallback to simple phase progression\n        phases = [\'EXPAND\', \'TYPE\', \'ENUMERATE\', \'CONSTRAIN\', \'COLLAPSE\', \'BIND\', \'EXECUTE\']\n        try:\n            current_idx = phases.index(current_phase)\n            if current_idx < len(phases) - 1:\n                return phases[current_idx + 1]\n        except ValueError:\n            pass\n        \n        return \'EXECUTE\'\n    \n    def update_weights(self, gdh_weight: float, uncertainty_weight: float):\n        """\n        Update weights for combining G/D/H and uncertainty scores\n        \n        Args:\n            gdh_weight: Weight for G/D/H score (0.0 to 1.0)\n            uncertainty_weight: Weight for uncertainty score (0.0 to 1.0)\n        """\n        total = gdh_weight + uncertainty_weight\n        self.weights[\'gdh\'] = gdh_weight / total\n        self.weights[\'uncertainty\'] = uncertainty_weight / total\n        \n        logger.info(f"Updated weights: G/D/H={self.weights[\'gdh\']:.2f}, "\n                   f"Uncertainty={self.weights[\'uncertainty\']:.2f}")\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Validate with unified confidence engine\n        confidence_report = self.confidence_engine.calculate_confidence(task, context)\n        \n        if not confidence_report.gate_result.approved:\n            logger.warning(\n                f"Task {task.get(\'id\')} rejected by Murphy Gate: "\n                f"{confidence_report.gate_result.reason}"\n            )\n            return ExecutionResult(\n                task_id=task.get(\'id\'),\n                status=ExecutionStatus.REJECTED,\n                message=confidence_report.gate_result.reason,\n                confidence_report=confidence_report,\n                timestamp=datetime.now()\n            )\n        \n        # Execute using original orchestrator if available\n        if self.orchestrator:\n            try:\n                result = await self._execute_with_orchestrator(task, exec_context)\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f"Error executing with orchestrator: {e}")\n                result = await self._execute_with_form_executor(task, exec_context)\n        else:\n            # Fallback to form executor\n            result = await self._execute_with_form_executor(task, exec_context)\n        \n        # Add confidence report to result\n        result.confidence_report = confidence_report\n        \n        logger.info(\n            f"Task {task.get(\'id\')} completed with status: {result.status}"\n        )\n        \n        return result\n    \n    async def _execute_with_orchestrator(\n        self,\n        task: Dict[str, Any],\n        context: ExecutionContext\n    ) -> ExecutionResult:\n        """\n        Execute task using original orchestrator\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task to execute\n            context: Execution context\n        \n        Returns:\n            Execution result\n        """\n        \n        logger.debug(f"Executing task {task.get(\'id\')} with original orchestrator")\n        \n        try:\n            # Check with HITL monitor\n        hitl_needs_intervention = self.hitl_monitor.check_checkpoint(\n            task, phase, context\n        )\n        \n        # Intervention needed if either system requests it\n        needs_intervention = supervisor_needs_intervention or hitl_needs_intervention\n        \n        if needs_intervention:\n            logger.info(\n                f"Intervention needed for task {task.get(\'id\')} at phase {phase} "\n                f"(supervisor: {supervisor_needs_intervention}, "\n                f"hitl: {hitl_needs_intervention})"\n            )\n        \n        return needs_intervention\n    \n    def request_intervention(\n        self,\n        task: Dict[str, Any],\n        checkpoint: HumanCheckpoint,\n        reason: str\n    ) -> InterventionRequest:\n        """\n        Request human intervention\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task requiring intervention\n            checkpoint: Checkpoint that triggered request\n            reason: Reason for intervention\n        \n        Returns:\n            Intervention request\n        """\n        \n        request = self.hitl_monitor.request_intervention(\n            task=task,\n            checkpoint=checkpoint,\n            reason=reason\n        )\n        \n        logger.info(\n            f"Intervention requested for task {task.get(\'id\')}: {reason}"\n        )\n        \n        # Notify original supervisor if available\n        if self.supervisor:\n            try:\n                self.supervisor.notify_intervention_requested(\n                    task_id=task.get(\'id\'),\n                    reason=reason\n                )\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f"Error notifying supervisor: {e}")\n        \n        return request\n    \n    def submit_intervention_response(\n        self,\n        request_id: str,\n        response_data: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> InterventionResponse:\n        """\n        Submit human response to intervention request\n        \n        Args:\n            request_id: Intervention request ID\n            response_data: Response data\n        \n        Returns:\n            Intervention response\n        """\n        \n        response = self.hitl_monitor.submit_response(\n            request_id=request_id,\n            response_data=response_data\n        )\n        \n        logger.info(\n            f"Intervention response submitted for request {request_id}: "\n            f"{response.decision}"\n        )\n        \n        # Notify original supervisor if available\n        if self.supervisor:\n            try:\n                self.supervisor.notify_intervention_completed(\n                    request_id=request_id,\n                    decision=response.decision\n                )\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f"Error notifying supervisor: {e}")\n        \n        return response\n    \n    def get_pending_interventions(self) -> List[InterventionRequest]:\n        """\n        Get all pending intervention requests\n        \n        Returns:\n            List of pending requests\n        """\n        \n        return self.hitl_monitor.get_pending_requests()\n    \n    def get_checkpoint_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Get checkpoint statistics\n        \n        Returns:\n            Statistics dictionary\n        """\n        \n        stats = self.hitl_monitor.get_statistics()\n        \n        # Unified Confidence Engine\n\n**Purpose:** Combines original G/D/H confidence with new UD/UA/UI/UR/UG uncertainty\n\n```python\nclass UnifiedConfidenceEngine:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Original system\n        self.confidence_calculator = ConfidenceCalculator()  # G/D/H\n        self.phase_controller = PhaseController()\n        \n        # New system\n        self.uncertainty_calculator = UncertaintyCalculator()  # UD/UA/UI/UR/UG\n        self.murphy_gate = MurphyGate()\n    \n    def calculate_confidence(self, task):\n        # Get both scores\n        gdh_score = self.confidence_calculator.calculate(task)\n        uncertainty_scores = self.uncertainty_calculator.calculate(task)\n        \n        # Combine with weighted average\n        combined = 0.5 * gdh_score + 0.5 * (1.0 - uncertainty_scores.total)\n        \n        # Apply Murphy Gate\n        gate_result = self.murphy_gate.evaluate(combined, uncertainty_scores)\n        \n        return ConfidenceReport(...)\n```\n\n### 2. Integrated Correction System\n\n**Purpose:** Captures corrections and feeds to original learning engine\n\n```python\nclass IntegratedCorrectionSystem:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Original learning system\n        self.learning_system = LearningSystem()\n        \n        # New correction capture\n        self.correction_recorder = CorrectionRecorder()\n        self.pattern_extractor = PatternExtractor()\n    \n    def capture_correction(self, task_id, correction_data):\n        # Record correction\n        correction = self.correction_recorder.record(...)\n        \n        # Extract patterns\n        patterns = self.pattern_extractor.extract(correction)\n        \n        # Feed to original learning engine\n        self.learning_system.learn_from_correction(patterns)\n```\n\n### 3. Integrated Form Executor\n\n**Purpose:** Executes form tasks using original execution orchestrator\n\n```python\nclass IntegratedFormExecutor:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Original execution system\n        self.orchestrator = ExecutionOrchestrator()\n        self.phase_controller = PhaseController()\n        \n        # Unified confidence engine\n        self.confidence_engine = UnifiedConfidenceEngine()\n    \n    async def execute_form_task(self, form_data):\n        # Convert form to task\n        task = self._form_to_task(form_data)\n        \n        # Validate with Murphy\n        validation = self.confidence_engine.calculate_confidence(task)\n        \n        if not validation.approved:\n            return {"status": "rejected"}\n        \n        # Execute with original orchestrator\n        result = await self.orchestrator.execute(task)\n        \n        return result\n```\n\n### 4. Integrated HITL Monitor\n\n**Purpose:** Combines new HITL checkpoints with original supervisor\n\n```python\nclass IntegratedHITLMonitor:\n    def __init__(self):\n        # Original supervisor\n        self.supervisor = Supervisor()\n        \n        # New HITL monitor\n        self.hitl_monitor = HumanInTheLoopMonitor()\n    \n    def check_intervention_needed(self, task, phase):\n        # Check both systems\n        supervisor_decision = self.supervisor.should_intervene(task)\n        hitl_decision = self.hitl_monitor.check_checkpoint(task, phase)\n        \n        # Intervention needed if either requests it\n        return supervisor_decision or hitl_decision\n```\n\n## Key Features\n\n### ✅ Backward Compatibility\n- All original 272 files preserved\n- All original endpoints functional\n- Original murphy_complete_backend.py unchanged\n- murphy_ui_final.html works as before\n\n### ✅ New Capabilities\n- Form-driven task submission\n- Enhanced confidence validation (G/D/H + Murphy)\n- Correction capture and pattern extraction\n- Shadow agent training pipeline\n- Human-in-the-loop checkpoints\n- Risk assessment and mitigation\n\n### ✅ Seamless Integration\n- Integration classes bridge old and new\n- Fallback to original system if new components unavailable\n- Weighted combination of confidence scores\n- Unified API surface\n\n## Testing Status\n\n### ✅ Completed\n- File copying and organization\n- Import path updates\n- Integration class creation\n- Backend endpoint creation\n\n### ⏳ Remaining\n- Unit tests for integration classes\n- End-to-end integration tests\n- Performance testing\n- UI integration\n- Documentation updates\n\n## Next Steps\n\n### Immediate (Phase 3)\n1. Open the UI\n\nOpen your browser and navigate to:\n```\nhttp://localhost:6666/murphy_ui_integrated.html\n```\n\nOr open the file directly:\n```bash\n# On Linux/Mac\nopen murphy_ui_integrated.html\n\n# On Windows\nstart murphy_ui_integrated.html\n```\n\n**Note:** If opening directly, update the API_BASE in the HTML file to point to your server:\n```javascript\nconst API_BASE = \'http://localhost:6666/api\';\n```\n\n## UI Features\n\n### 📝 Form Submission Tab\nSubmit tasks with automatic Murphy validation:\n- Select task type (general, data processing, analysis, generation)\n- Provide task description\n- Add parameters in JSON format\n- View confidence scores and execution results\n\n### ✓ Validation Tab\nValidate tasks without executing them:\n- Test task data before execution\n- See detailed uncertainty scores (UD, UA, UI, UR, UG)\n- Get approval/rejection decisions with reasons\n\n### 🔧 Corrections Tab\nHelp Murphy learn from corrections:\n- Submit corrections for completed tasks\n- Specify correction type\n- Provide original and corrected outputs\n- View correction statistics\n\n### 📊 Monitoring Tab\nReal-time system statistics:\n- Total tasks executed\n- Number of corrections submitted\n- Average confidence scores\n- Success rates\n\n## API Endpoints\n\n### Form Endpoints\n- `POST /api/forms/plan-upload` - Upload pre-existing plan\n- `POST /api/forms/plan-generation` - Generate plan from description\n- `POST /api/forms/task-execution` - Execute task with Murphy validation\n- `POST /api/forms/validation` - Validate task without executing\n- `POST /api/forms/correction` - Submit correction\n- `GET /api/forms/submission/<id>` - Get submission status\n\n### Correction Endpoints\n- `GET /api/corrections/patterns` - Get extracted patterns\n- `GET /api/corrections/statistics` - Get correction statistics\n- `GET /api/corrections/training-data` - Get shadow agent training data\n\n### HITL Endpoints\n- `GET /api/hitl/interventions/pending` - Get pending interventions\n- `POST /api/hitl/interventions/<id>/respond` - Respond to intervention\n- `GET /api/hitl/statistics` - Get HITL statistics\n\n### System Info\n- `GET /api/system/info` - Get integrated system information\n\n## Example Usage\n\n### 1. Submit a Task\n\n**Via UI:**\n1. Go to "Form Submission" tab\n2. Select task type: "General Task"\n3. Enter description: "Analyze sales data for Q4"\n4. Add parameters: `{"quarter": "Q4", "year": 2024}`\n5. Click "Execute Task"\n\n**Via API:**\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:6666/api/forms/task-execution \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "task_type": "analysis",\n    "description": "Analyze sales data for Q4",\n    "parameters": {"quarter": "Q4", "year": 2024}\n  }\'\n```\n\n### 2. Validate a Task\n\n**Via UI:**\n1. Go to "Validation" tab\n2. Enter task data:\n```json\n{\n  "task_type": "general",\n  "description": "Process customer data",\n  "parameters": {}\n}\n```\n3. Click "Validate"\n4. View confidence scores and approval decision\n\n**Via API:**\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:6666/api/forms/validation \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "task_data": {\n      "task_type": "general",\n      "description": "Process customer data"\n    }\n  }\'\n```\n\n### 3. Submit a Correction\n\n**Via UI:**\n1. Go to "Corrections" tab\n2. Enter task ID: "task_12345"\n3. Select correction type: "Output Error"\n4. Enter original output: "Wrong result"\n5. Enter corrected output: "Correct result"\n6. Add explanation: "Fixed calculation error"\n7. Click "Submit Correction"\n\n**Via API:**\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:6666/api/forms/correction \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "task_id": "task_12345",\n    "correction_type": "output_error",\n    "original_output": "Wrong result",\n    "corrected_output": "Correct result",\n    "explanation": "Fixed calculation error"\n  }\'\n```\n\n### 4. View Statistics\n\n**Via UI:**\n1. Go to "Monitoring" tab\n2. Click "Refresh Statistics"\n3. View real-time metrics\n\n**Via API:**\n```bash\n# Correction statistics\ncurl http://localhost:6666/api/corrections/statistics\n\n# HITL statistics\ncurl http://localhost:6666/api/hitl/statistics\n\n# System info\ncurl http://localhost:6666/api/system/info\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Server won\'t start\n- Check if port 6666 is already in use\n- Verify all dependencies are installed: `pip install -r requirements.txt`\n- Check Python version (3.11+ recommended)\n\n### UI can\'t connect to server\n- Verify server is running on http://localhost:6666\n- Check browser console for CORS errors\n- Ensure API_BASE in HTML matches server URL\n\n### Import errors\n- Run the import test: `python tests/test_basic_imports.py`\n- All 5 tests should pass\n- If not, check that you\'re in the murphy_integrated directory\n\n## Next Steps\n\n1. **Test the system** - Try submitting tasks and corrections\n2. **Monitor performance** - Check the monitoring tab regularly\n3. **Review corrections** - See what Murphy is learning\n4. **Integrate with existing workflows** - Use the API endpoints\n\n## Support\n\nFor issues or questions:\n1. {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_integrated/API_DOCUMENTATION.md">\n# Murphy System - Complete API Documentation\n\n## Base URL\n```\nhttp://localhost:6666/api\n```\n\n## Authentication\nCurrently, no authentication is required. In production, implement appropriate authentication mechanisms.\n\n---\n\n## Form Endpoints\n\n### 1. Upload Plan\nUpload a pre-existing plan for execution.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/plan-upload`\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "plan_name": "string",\n  "plan_data": {\n    "tasks": [...],\n    "dependencies": [...]\n  },\n  "format": "json|yaml|markdown"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "submission_id": "sub_12345",\n  "plan_id": "plan_67890",\n  "tasks_count": 5,\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-01T12:00:00"\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `400` - Invalid request data\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 2. Generate Plan\nGenerate a plan from natural language description.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/plan-generation`\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "description": "string",\n  "domain": "string",\n  "constraints": ["constraint1", "constraint2"],\n  "preferences": {\n    "priority": "speed|quality",\n    "max_tasks": 10\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "submission_id": "sub_12345",\n  "plan_id": "plan_67890",\n  "generated_plan": {\n    "tasks": [...],\n    "dependencies": [...]\n  },\n  "tasks_count": 5,\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-01T12:00:00"\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `400` - Invalid request data\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 3. Execute Task\nExecute a task with Murphy validation.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/task-execution`\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_type": "general|data_processing|analysis|generation",\n  "description": "string",\n  "parameters": {\n    "key": "value"\n  },\n  "constraints": ["constraint1"],\n  "validation_required": true\n}\n```\n\n**Response (Success):**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "task_id": "task_12345",\n  "status": "COMPLETED",\n  "output": {\n    "result": "..."\n  },\n  "confidence_report": {\n    "combined_confidence": 0.85,\n    "uncertainty_scores": {\n      "UD": 0.1,\n      "UA": 0.15,\n      "UI": 0.05,\n      "UR": 0.1,\n      "UG": 0.05,\n      "total": 0.45\n    }\n  },\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-01T12:00:00"\n}\n```\n\n**Response (Rejected):**\n```json\n{\n  "success": false,\n  "status": "rejected",\n  "reason": "Confidence too low (0.45 < 0.60)",\n  "confidence_report": {\n    "combined_confidence": 0.45,\n    "uncertainty_scores": {...},\n    "gate_result": {\n      "approved": false,\n      "reason": "High uncertainty in data and resources"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `403` - Task rejected by Murphy Gate\n- `400` - Invalid request data\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 4. Validate Task\nValidate a task without executing it.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/validation`\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_data": {\n    "task_type": "general",\n    "description": "string",\n    "parameters": {}\n  },\n  "validation_criteria": ["criterion1"]\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "approved": true,\n  "confidence": 0.85,\n  "gdh_confidence": 0.80,\n  "uncertainty_scores": {\n    "UD": 0.1,\n    "UA": 0.15,\n    "UI": 0.05,\n    "UR": 0.1,\n    "UG": 0.05,\n    "total": 0.45\n  },\n  "gate_result": {\n    "approved": true,\n    "reason": "All validation criteria met",\n    "recommendations": ["Monitor execution closely"]\n  },\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-01T12:00:00"\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `400` - Invalid request data\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 5. Submit Correction\nSubmit a correction for a completed task.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/correction`\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_id": "task_12345",\n  "correction_type": "output_error|parameter_adjustment|logic_correction|validation_override",\n  "original_output": "string or object",\n  "corrected_output": "string or object",\n  "explanation": "string",\n  "severity": "low|medium|high|critical"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "correction_id": "corr_67890",\n  "task_id": "task_12345",\n  "patterns_extracted": 3,\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-01T12:00:00"\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `400` - Invalid request data\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 6. Get Submission Status\nGet the status of a form submission.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/forms/submission/{submission_id}`\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "submission": {\n    "id": "sub_12345",\n    "type": "task_execution",\n    "status": "completed|pending|failed",\n    "created_at": "2024-01-01T12:00:00",\n    "completed_at": "2024-01-01T12:05:00",\n    "result": {...}\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `404` - Submission not found\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n## Correction Endpoints\n\n### 7. Get Correction Patterns\nGet extracted correction patterns.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/corrections/patterns`\n\n**Query Parameters:**\n- `task_type` (optional) - Filter by task type\n- `min_frequency` (optional, default: 2) - Minimum pattern frequency\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "patterns": [\n    {\n      "pattern_id": "pat_12345",\n      "pattern_type": "frequent_correction",\n      "description": "Common parameter adjustment",\n      "frequency": 15,\n      "confidence": 0.85,\n      "examples": [...]\n    }\n  ],\n  "count": 10\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 8. Get Correction Statistics\nGet correction system statistics.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/corrections/statistics`\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "statistics": {\n    "total_corrections": 150,\n    "total_patterns": 25,\n    "corrections_by_type": {\n      "output_error": 80,\n      "parameter_adjustment": 40,\n      "logic_correction": 20,\n      "validation_override": 10\n    },\n    "corrections_by_severity": {\n      "low": 50,\n      "medium": 70,\n      "high": 25,\n      "critical": 5\n    },\n    "patterns_by_type": {\n      "frequent_correction": 10,\n      "common_error": 8,\n      "systematic_issue": 7\n    },\n    "has_learning_system": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 9. Get Training Data\nGet training data for shadow agent.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/corrections/training-data`\n\n**Query Parameters:**\n- `task_type` (optional) - Filter by task type\n- `limit` (optional) - Maximum number of examples\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "training_data": [\n    {\n      "task_id": "task_12345",\n      "original_output": "...",\n      "corrected_output": "...",\n      "correction_type": "output_error",\n      "metadata": {...},\n      "timestamp": "2024-01-01T12:00:00"\n    }\n  ],\n  "count": 50\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n## HITL (Human-in-the-Loop) Endpoints\n\n### 10. Get Pending Interventions\nGet all pending intervention requests.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/hitl/interventions/pending`\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "interventions": [\n    {\n      "request_id": "int_12345",\n      "task_id": "task_67890",\n      "intervention_type": "approval_required",\n      "urgency": "high",\n      "reason": "High-risk operation detected",\n      "created_at": "2024-01-01T12:00:00",\n      "status": "pending"\n    }\n  ],\n  "count": 5\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 11. Respond to Intervention\nRespond to an intervention request.\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/hitl/interventions/{request_id}/respond`\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "decision": "approve|reject|modify",\n  "comments": "string",\n  "modifications": {\n    "parameter": "new_value"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "response": {\n    "request_id": "int_12345",\n    "decision": "approve",\n    "responded_by": "user_id",\n    "responded_at": "2024-01-01T12:05:00",\n    "comments": "Approved after review"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `404` - Intervention not found\n- `400` - Invalid request data\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n### 12. Get HITL Statistics\nGet HITL checkpoint statistics.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/hitl/statistics`\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "statistics": {\n    "total_interventions": 100,\n    "pending_interventions": 5,\n    "approved": 80,\n    "rejected": 15,\n    "average_response_time": "5m 30s",\n    "by_type": {\n      "approval_required": 60,\n      "review_requested": 30,\n      "clarification_needed": 10\n    },\n    "supervisor": {\n      "total_supervisions": 500,\n      "interventions_triggered": 100\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n- `500` - Server error\n\n---\n\n## System Endpoints\n\n### 13. Get System Info\nGet integrated system information.\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/system/info`\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "system": {\n    "name": "Murphy System - Integrated",\n    "version": "2.0.0",\n    "components": {\n      "murphy_runtime": true,\n      "domain_engine": true,\n      "form_intake": true,\n      "murphy_validation": true,\n      "correction_capture": true,\n      "shadow_agent": true,\n      "hitl_monitor": true\n    },\n    "endpoints": {\n      "original": "All original endpoints preserved",\n      "forms": "/api/forms/*",\n      "corrections": "/api/corrections/*",\n      "hitl": "/api/hitl/*",\n      "system": "/api/system/*"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200` - Success\n\n---\n\n## Error Responses\n\nAll endpoints may return error responses in the following format:\n\n```json\n{\n  "success": false,\n  "error": "Error message describing what went wrong",\n  "details": {\n    "field": "Additional error details"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Common Error Codes:**\n- `400` - Bad Request (invalid input)\n- `403` - Forbidden (rejected by Murphy Gate)\n- `404` - Not Found\n- `500` - Internal Server Error\n\n---\n\n## Rate Limiting\n\nCurrently, no rate limiting is implemented. In production, consider implementing:\n- Rate limiting per IP/user\n- Request throttling\n- Queue management for long-running tasks\n\n---\n\n## Webhooks (Future)\n\nFuture versions may support webhooks for:\n- Task completion notifications\n- Intervention requests\n- Pattern detection alerts\n- System health updates\n\n---\n\n## SDK Examples\n\n### Python\n```python\nimport requests\n\nAPI_BASE = "http://localhost:6666/api"\n\n# Execute a task\nresponse = requests.post(\n    f"{API_BASE}/forms/task-execution",\n    json={\n        "task_type": "analysis",\n        "description": "Analyze sales data",\n        "parameters": {"quarter": "Q4"}\n    }\n)\n\nresult = response.json()\nprint(f"Task ID: {result[\'task_id\']}")\nprint(f"Confidence: {result[\'confidence_report\'][\'combined_confidence\']}")\n```\n\n### JavaScript\n```javascript\nconst API_BASE = \'http://localhost:6666/api\';\n\n// Execute a task\nasync function executeTask() {\n  const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/forms/task-execution`, {\n    method: \'POST\',\n    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n    body: JSON.stringify({\n      task_type: \'analysis\',\n      description: \'Analyze sales data\',\n      parameters: { quarter: \'Q4\' }\n    })\n  });\n  \n  const result = await response.json();\n  console.log(\'Task ID:\', result.task_id);\n  console.log(\'Confidence:\', result.confidence_report.combined_confidence);\n}\n```\n\n### cURL\n```bash\n# Execute a task\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:6666/api/forms/task-execution \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "task_type": "analysis",\n    "description": "Analyze sales data",\n    "parameters": {"quarter": "Q4"}\n  }\'\n```\n\n---\n\n## Best Practices\n\n1. **Always validate tasks** before execution in production\n2. **Monitor confidence scores** - reject tasks with confidence < 0.60\n3. **Submit corrections** to improve system learning\n4. **Handle interventions promptly** to avoid blocking\n5. **Use appropriate task types** for better validation\n6. **Provide detailed descriptions** for better results\n7. **Check system info** to verify component availability\n\n---\n\n## Support\n\nFor API issues or questions:\n- Check the START_INTEGRATED_SYSTEM.md guide\n- Review integration documentation\n- Test with the provided UI at murphy_ui_integrated.html\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Clone/Extract the Repository\n```bash\n# If from zip\nunzip murphy_integrated.zip\ncd murphy_integrated\n\n# If from git\ngit clone <repository-url>\ncd murphy_integrated\n```\n\n### 2. Create Virtual Environment\n```bash\n# Create virtual environment\npython -m venv venv\n\n# Activate virtual environment\n# On Linux/Mac:\nsource venv/bin/activate\n\n# On Windows:\nvenv\\Scripts\\activate\n```\n\n### 3. Install Dependencies\n```bash\n# Install Python dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Verify installation\npython tests/test_basic_imports.py\n```\n\nExpected output:\n```\n✓ UnifiedConfidenceEngine imported successfully\n✓ IntegratedCorrectionSystem imported successfully\n✓ IntegratedFormExecutor imported successfully\n✓ IntegratedHITLMonitor imported successfully\n✓ Form intake modules imported successfully\n\nResults: 5/5 tests passed\n```\n\n### 4. Start the Server\n```bash\n# Start the integrated backend\npython murphy_complete_backend_extended.py\n```\n\nServer will start on: **http://localhost:6666**\n\n### 5. Access the UI\nOpen your browser and navigate to:\n```\nhttp://localhost:6666/murphy_ui_integrated.html\n```\n\n---\n\n## Production Deployment\n\n### 1. Prepare Production Environment\n\n#### Update Configuration\nCreate `config_production.py`:\n```python\n# Production configuration\nDEBUG = False\nHOST = \'0.0.0.0\'\nPORT = 6666\nWORKERS = 4\n\n# Security\nSECRET_KEY = \'your-secret-key-here\'\nALLOWED_ORIGINS = [\'https://yourdomain.com\']\n\n# Database (if using)\nDATABASE_URL = \'postgresql://user:pass@localhost/murphy\'\n\n# Logging\nLOG_LEVEL = \'INFO\'\nLOG_FILE = \'/var/log/murphy/murphy.log\'\n```\n\n#### Set Environment Variables\n```bash\nexport MURPHY_ENV=production\nexport MURPHY_SECRET_KEY=your-secret-key\nexport MURPHY_DATABASE_URL=postgresql://...\n```\n\n### 2. Use Production WSGI Server\n\n#### Install Gunicorn\n```bash\npip install gunicorn\n```\n\n#### Start with Gunicorn\n```bash\ngunicorn -w 4 -b 0.0.0.0:6666 \\\n  --timeout 120 \\\n  --access-logfile /var/log/murphy/access.log \\\n  --error-logfile /var/log/murphy/error.log \\\n  murphy_complete_backend_extended:app\n```\n\n### 3. Setup Nginx Reverse Proxy\n\n#### Install Nginx\n```bash\n# Ubuntu/Debian\nsudo apt-get install nginx\n\n# CentOS/RHEL\nsudo yum install nginx\n```\n\n#### Configure Nginx\nCreate `/etc/nginx/sites-available/murphy`:\n```nginx\nserver {\n    listen 80;\n    server_name yourdomain.com;\n\n    location / {\n        proxy_pass http://127.0.0.1:6666;\n        proxy_set_header Host $host;\n        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;\n        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;\n        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;\n        \n        # WebSocket support (if needed)\n        proxy_http_version 1.1;\n        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;\n        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";\n        \n        # Timeouts\n        proxy_connect_timeout 120s;\n        proxy_send_timeout 120s;\n        proxy_read_timeout 120s;\n    }\n\n    # Static files\n    location /static {\n        alias /path/to/murphy_integrated/static;\n        expires 30d;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nEnable the site:\n```bash\nsudo ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/murphy /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/\nsudo nginx -t\nsudo systemctl restart nginx\n```\n\n### 4. Setup SSL with Let\'s Encrypt\n```bash\n# Install certbot\nsudo apt-get install certbot python3-certbot-nginx\n\n# Get certificate\nsudo certbot --nginx -d yourdomain.com\n\n# Auto-renewal\nsudo certbot renew --dry-run\n```\n\n### 5. Create Systemd Service\n\nCreate `/etc/systemd/system/murphy.service`:\n```ini\n[Unit]\nDescription=Murphy System Integrated Backend\nAfter=network.target\n\n[Service]\nType=notify\nUser=murphy\nGroup=murphy\nWorkingDirectory=/opt/murphy_integrated\nEnvironment="PATH=/opt/murphy_integrated/venv/bin"\nExecStart=/opt/murphy_integrated/venv/bin/gunicorn \\\n    -w 4 \\\n    -b 127.0.0.1:6666 \\\n    --timeout 120 \\\n    --access-logfile /var/log/murphy/access.log \\\n    --error-logfile /var/log/murphy/error.log \\\n    murphy_complete_backend_extended:app\n\nRestart=always\nRestartSec=10\n\n[Install]\nWantedBy=multi-user.target\n```\n\nEnable and start:\n```bash\nsudo systemctl daemon-reload\nsudo systemctl enable murphy\nsudo systemctl start murphy\nsudo systemctl status murphy\n```\n\n---\n\n## Docker Deployment\n\n### 1. Create Dockerfile\n```dockerfile\nFROM python:3.11-slim\n\nWORKDIR /app\n\n# Install system dependencies\nRUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \\\n    gcc \\\n    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*\n\n# Copy requirements and install\nCOPY requirements.txt .\nRUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt\n\n# Copy application\nCOPY . .\n\n# Create non-root user\nRUN useradd -m -u 1000 murphy && \\\n    chown -R murphy:murphy /app\nUSER murphy\n\n# Expose port\nEXPOSE 6666\n\n# Health check\nHEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \\\n    CMD python -c "import requests; requests.get(\'http://localhost:6666/api/system/info\')"\n\n# Start application\nCMD ["gunicorn", "-w", "4", "-b", "0.0.0.0:6666", "--timeout", "120", "murphy_complete_backend_extended:app"]\n```\n\n### 2. Create docker-compose.yml\n```yaml\nversion: \'3.8\'\n\nservices:\n  murphy:\n    build: .\n    ports:\n      - "6666:6666"\n    environment:\n      - MURPHY_ENV=production\n      - MURPHY_SECRET_KEY=${MURPHY_SECRET_KEY}\n    volumes:\n      - ./logs:/app/logs\n      - ./data:/app/data\n    restart: unless-stopped\n    healthcheck:\n      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:6666/api/system/info"]\n      interval: 30s\n      timeout: 10s\n      retries: 3\n      start_period: 40s\n\n  nginx:\n    image: nginx:alpine\n    ports:\n      - "80:80"\n      - "443:443"\n    volumes:\n      - ./nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro\n      - ./ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro\n    depends_on:\n      - murphy\n    restart: unless-stopped\n\nvolumes:\n  logs:\n  data:\n```\n\n### 3. Build and Run\n```bash\n# Build image\ndocker build -t murphy-system:latest .\n\n# Run with docker-compose\ndocker-compose up -d\n\n# View logs\ndocker-compose logs -f murphy\n\n# Stop\ndocker-compose down\n```\n\n---\n\n## Kubernetes Deployment\n\n### 1. Create Deployment\n`murphy-deployment.yaml`:\n```yaml\napiVersion: apps/v1\nkind: Deployment\nmetadata:\n  name: murphy-system\n  labels:\n    app: murphy\nspec:\n  replicas: 3\n  selector:\n    matchLabels:\n      app: murphy\n  template:\n    metadata:\n      labels:\n        app: murphy\n    spec:\n      containers:\n      - name: murphy\n        image: murphy-system:latest\n        ports:\n        - containerPort: 6666\n        env:\n        - name: MURPHY_ENV\n          value: "production"\n        - name: MURPHY_SECRET_KEY\n          valueFrom:\n            secretKeyRef:\n              name: murphy-secrets\n              key: secret-key\n        resources:\n          requests:\n            memory: "512Mi"\n            cpu: "500m"\n          limits:\n            memory: "2Gi"\n            cpu: "2000m"\n        livenessProbe:\n          httpGet:\n            path: /api/system/info\n            port: 6666\n          initialDelaySeconds: 30\n          periodSeconds: 10\n        readinessProbe:\n          httpGet:\n            path: /api/system/info\n            port: 6666\n          initialDelaySeconds: 5\n          periodSeconds: 5\n```\n\n### 2. Create Service\n`murphy-service.yaml`:\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: Service\nmetadata:\n  name: murphy-service\nspec:\n  selector:\n    app: murphy\n  ports:\n  - protocol: TCP\n    port: 80\n    targetPort: 6666\n  type: LoadBalancer\n```\n\n### 3. Create HorizontalPodAutoscaler\n`murphy-hpa.yaml`:\n```yaml\napiVersion: autoscaling/v2\nkind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler\nmetadata:\n  name: murphy-hpa\nspec:\n  scaleTargetRef:\n    apiVersion: apps/v1\n    kind: Deployment\n    name: murphy-system\n  minReplicas: 3\n  maxReplicas: 10\n  metrics:\n  - type: Resource\n    resource:\n      name: cpu\n      target:\n        type: Utilization\n        averageUtilization: 70\n  - type: Resource\n    resource:\n      name: memory\n      target:\n        type: Utilization\n        averageUtilization: 80\n```\n\n### 4. Deploy to Kubernetes\n```bash\n# Create namespace\nkubectl create namespace murphy\n\n# Create secrets\nkubectl create secret generic murphy-secrets \\\n  --from-literal=secret-key=your-secret-key \\\n  -n murphy\n\n# Apply configurations\nkubectl apply -f murphy-deployment.yaml -n murphy\nkubectl apply -f murphy-service.yaml -n murphy\nkubectl apply -f murphy-hpa.yaml -n murphy\n\n# Check status\nkubectl get pods -n murphy\nkubectl get svc -n murphy\n\n# View logs\nkubectl logs -f deployment/murphy-system -n murphy\n```\n\n---\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Environment Variables\n```bash\n# Application\nMURPHY_ENV=production|development\nMURPHY_DEBUG=false\nMURPHY_HOST=0.0.0.0\nMURPHY_PORT=6666\n\n# Security\nMURPHY_SECRET_KEY=your-secret-key\nMURPHY_ALLOWED_ORIGINS=https://yourdomain.com\n\n# Database (optional)\nMURPHY_DATABASE_URL=postgresql://user:pass@host/db\n\n# Logging\nMURPHY_LOG_LEVEL=INFO|DEBUG|WARNING|ERROR\nMURPHY_LOG_FILE=/var/log/murphy/murphy.log\n\n# Performance\nMURPHY_WORKERS=4\nMURPHY_TIMEOUT=120\n```\n\n### Configuration File\nCreate `config.yaml`:\n```yaml\nserver:\n  host: 0.0.0.0\n  port: 6666\n  workers: 4\n  timeout: 120\n\nsecurity:\n  secret_key: ${MURPHY_SECRET_KEY}\n  allowed_origins:\n    - https://yourdomain.com\n  cors_enabled: true\n\nlogging:\n  level: INFO\n  file: /var/log/murphy/murphy.log\n  format: "%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"\n\nfeatures:\n  form_intake: true\n  murphy_validation: true\n  correction_capture: true\n  shadow_agent: true\n  hitl_monitor: true\n```\n\n---\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### 1. Form-Driven Task Execution\n- Submit tasks via forms (JSON, YAML, or natural language)\n- Automatic task decomposition\n- Dependency management\n- Async execution with progress tracking\n\n#### 2. Murphy Validation System\n- **Original G/D/H Formula** - Goodness, Domain, Hazard scoring\n- **New 5D Uncertainty** - UD (Data), UA (Authority), UI (Information), UR (Resources), UG (Disagreement)\n- **Murphy Gate** - Threshold-based approval/rejection\n- **Confidence Reports** - Detailed validation results\n\n#### 3. Correction Capture & Learning\n- **4 Capture Methods** - Interactive, batch, API, inline\n- **Pattern Extraction** - Automatic learning from corrections\n- **Feedback System** - Collect and analyze human feedback\n- **Validation** - Conflict detection and quality scoring\n\n#### 4. Shadow Agent Training\n- **Training Pipeline** - Automated data preparation and model training\n- **Continuous Learning** - Learns from every correction\n- **A/B Testing** - Compare shadow agent vs Murphy Gate\n- **Gradual Rollout** - Safe production deployment\n\n#### 5. Human-in-the-Loop (HITL)\n- **Smart Checkpoints** - 6 checkpoint types for critical decisions\n- **Intervention Requests** - Automatic escalation when needed\n- **Approval Workflows** - Structured decision-making\n- **Statistics** - Track intervention patterns\n\n---\n\n## 🏗️ Architecture\n\n### System Components\n\n```\nmurphy_integrated/\n├── src/\n│   ├── form_intake/              # Form processing (6 files)\n│   ├── confidence_engine/        # Validation (+23 files)\n│   │   ├── unified_confidence_engine.py  # Integration class\n│   │   ├── uncertainty_calculator.py     # 5D uncertainty\n│   │   ├── murphy_gate.py                # Threshold validation\n│   │   └── risk/                         # Risk assessment\n│   ├── execution_engine/         # Task execution (+8 files)\n│   │   └── integrated_form_executor.py   # Integration class\n│   ├── learning_engine/          # Learning & corrections (+22 files)\n│   │   ├── integrated_correction_system.py  # Integration class\n│   │   ├── correction_capture.py            # Capture system\n│   │   ├── pattern_extraction.py            # Pattern mining\n│   │   └── shadow_agent.py                  # Self-improving AI\n│   ├── supervisor_system/        # HITL monitoring (+8 files)\n│   │   └── integrated_hitl_monitor.py    # Integration class\n│   └── ... "task_data": {\n      "task_type": "general",\n      "description": "Process customer data"\n    }\n  }\'\n```\n\n#### Submit a Correction\n```bash\ncurl -X POST /api/hitl/interventions/pending` - Get pending interventions\n- `POST /api/hitl/interventions/<id>/respond` - Respond to intervention\n- `GET /api/hitl/statistics` - Get HITL statistics\n\n**System Endpoints:**\n- `GET /api/system/info` - Get system information\n\n---\n\n## 🛠️ Development\n\n### Project Structure\n```\nmurphy_integrated/\n├── src/                          # Source code\n│   ├── Form-Driven Task Execution\n- Submit tasks via forms (JSON, YAML, or natural language)\n- Automatic task decomposition\n- Dependency management\n- Async execution with progress tracking\n\n#### 2. Murphy Validation System\n- **Original G/D/H Formula** - Goodness, Domain, Hazard scoring\n- **New 5D Uncertainty** - UD (Data), UA (Authority), UI (Information), UR (Resources), UG (Disagreement)\n- **Murphy Gate** - Threshold-based approval/rejection\n- **Confidence Reports** - Detailed validation results\n\n#### 3. Correction Capture & Learning\n- **4 Capture Methods** - Interactive, batch, API, inline\n- **Pattern Extraction** - Automatic learning from corrections\n- **Feedback System** - Collect and analyze human feedback\n- **Validation** - Conflict detection and quality scoring\n\n#### 4. Shadow Agent Training\n- **Training Pipeline** - Automated data preparation and model training\n- **Continuous Learning** - Learns from every correction\n- **A/B Testing** - Compare shadow agent vs Murphy Gate\n- **Gradual Rollout** - Safe production deployment\n\n#### 5. Human-in-the-Loop (HITL)\n- **Smart Checkpoints** - 6 checkpoint types for critical decisions\n- **Intervention Requests** - Automatic escalation when needed\n- **Approval Workflows** - Structured decision-making\n- **Statistics** - Track intervention patterns\n\n---\n\n## 🏗️ Architecture\n\n### System Components\n\n```\nmurphy_integrated/\n├── src/\n│   ├── form_intake/              # Form processing (6 files)\n│   ├── confidence_engine/        # Validation (+23 files)\n│   │   ├── unified_confidence_engine.py  # Integration class\n│   │   ├── uncertainty_calculator.py     # 5D uncertainty\n│   │   ├── murphy_gate.py                # Threshold validation\n│   │   └── risk/                         # Risk assessment\n│   ├── execution_engine/         # Task execution (+8 files)\n│   │   └── integrated_form_executor.py   # Integration class\n│   ├── learning_engine/          # Learning & corrections (+22 files)\n│   │   ├── integrated_correction_system.py  # Integration class\n│   │   ├── correction_capture.py            # Capture system\n│   │   ├── pattern_extraction.py            # Pattern mining\n│   │   └── shadow_agent.py                  # Self-improving AI\n│   ├── supervisor_system/        # HITL monitoring (+8 files)\n│   │   └── integrated_hitl_monitor.py    # Integration class\n│   └── ... Execute tasks with Murphy validation\n2. **✓ Validation** - Validate tasks without executing\n3. **🔧 Corrections** - Submit corrections to help Murphy learn\n4. **📊 Monitoring** - View system statistics and performance\n\n### API Usage\n\n#### Execute a Task\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:6666/api/forms/task-execution \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "task_type": "analysis",\n    "description": "Analyze Q4 sales data",\n    "parameters": {"quarter": "Q4", "year": 2024}\n  }\'\n```\n\n#### Validate a Task\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:6666/api/forms/validation \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "task_data": {\n      "task_type": "general",\n      "description": "Process customer data"\n    }\n  }\'\n```\n\n#### Submit a Correction\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:6666/api/forms/correction \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "task_id": "task_12345",\n    "correction_type": "output_error",\n    "original_output": "Wrong result",\n    "corrected_output": "Correct result",\n    "explanation": "Fixed calculation error"\n  }\'\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📚 API Documentation\n\nSee [API_DOCUMENTATION.md](API_DOCUMENTATION.md) for complete API reference.\n\n### Available Endpoints\n\n**Form Endpoints:**\n- `POST /api/forms/plan-upload` - Upload plan\n- `POST /api/forms/plan-generation` - Generate plan\n- `POST /api/forms/task-execution` - Execute task\n- `POST /api/forms/validation` - Validate task\n- `POST /api/forms/correction` - Submit correction\n- `GET /api/forms/submission/<id>` - Get submission status\n\n**Correction Endpoints:**\n- `GET /api/corrections/patterns` - Get patterns\n- `GET /api/corrections/statistics` - Get statistics\n- `GET /api/corrections/training-data` - Get training data\n\n**HITL Endpoints:**\n- `GET /api/hitl/interventions/pending` - Get pending interventions\n- `POST /api/hitl/interventions/<id>/respond` - Respond to intervention\n- `GET /api/hitl/statistics` - Get HITL statistics\n\n**System Endpoints:**\n- `GET /api/system/info` - Get system information\n\n---\n\n## 🛠️ Development\n\n### Running Tests\n```bash\n# Import tests\npython tests/test_basic_imports.py\n\n# Integration tests (requires pytest)\npip install pytest pytest-asyncio\npytest tests/test_integration.py -v\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 Deployment\n\nSee [DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE.md](DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE.md) for detailed deployment instructions.\n\n### Quick Deploy with Docker\n\n```bash\n# Build image\ndocker build -t murphy-system:latest .\n\n# Run container\ndocker run -d -p 6666:6666 murphy-system:latest\n```\n\n---\n\n## 📄 License\n\nCopyright © 2020 Inoni Limited Liability Company  \nCreator: Corey Post  \nLicense: Apache License 2.0\n\n---\n\n## 📞 Support\n\n### Documentation\n- [START_INTEGRATED_SYSTEM.md](START_INTEGRATED_SYSTEM.md) -
